TC_01_01.01_Update native Ad(Normal Method)
    Generate JSON For Creative Native           campaign_id=${Campaign_Id1}
    ...                                         adName="${CREATIVE_NAME}_NATIVE0101"
    CREATIVE POST Request for Creative          uri=native      JSON=${data}               expected_status_code=200
    Set Suite Variable                          ${nativeCreativeId}                      ${DTO_id}
    Create ad for Native            adgroupId=${nativeAdgroupId}                   creativeId=${nativeCreativeId}
    ...                             adName="${CREATIVE_NAME}_NATIVE0101_UP"

    Update ad for Native            adName="${CREATIVE_NAME}_NATIVE0101"
    Json Value Should Equal     ${body}         /success            true
    Json Value Should Equal     ${body}         /reason_desc        "Success"

    Set Suite Variable                          ${nativeCreativeId}                      ${DTO_id}
    Create ad for Native            adgroupId=${nativeAdgroupId}                   creativeId=${nativeCreativeId}
    ...                             adName="${CREATIVE_NAME}_NATIVE1409"
    Update ad for Native            adName="${CREATIVE_NAME}_NATIVE1409"
    ...               deleteFromUI=null
    ...                                 expected_status_code=200
    Json Value Should Equal     ${body}         /success            true
    Json Value Should Equal     ${body}         /reason_desc        "Success"
    [Tags]

TC_01_16.02_Update native Ad(Catalina user externalId blank)
    Generate JSON For Creative Native           campaign_id=${Campaign_Id_CAT}
    ...                                         adName="${CREATIVE_NAME}_NATIVE1602"

    CREATIVE POST Request for Creative          uri=native      JSON=${data}               expected_status_code=200
    Set Suite Variable                          ${nativeCreativeId}                      ${DTO_id}

	#This portion extract the native ad ID, to be used later
    ${DTO_ad_id}=    Get Json Value         ${body}         /creativeDetailDTO/nativeDTO/nativeAdId
	Log 	${DTO_ad_id}
	Set Suite Variable    ${DTO_ad_id}     ${DTO_ad_id}

    Create ad for Native            adgroupId=${nativeAdgroupId_CAT}                   creativeId=${nativeCreativeId}
    ...                             adName="${CREATIVE_NAME}_NATIVE1602"
    ...    auth=${QA_CATALINA_AUTH}

    #DTO_id, DTO_ad_id is generated from created ad
    Update ad for Native            adName="${CREATIVE_NAME}_NATIVE1602"
    ...        	auth=${QA_CATALINA_AUTH}
    ...			adgroupId=${nativeAdgroupId_CAT}
    ...    		creativeId=${DTO_id}
    ...			nativeAdId=${DTO_ad_id}
    ...			externalId=""
    ...			expected_status_code=400
    Json Value Should Equal     ${body}         /reason_code        "400-999"
    Json Value Should Equal     ${body}         /reason_desc        "Validation Failure"
    Json Value Should Equal     ${body}         /errors/0/field       	 	"nativeDTO.externalId"
	Json Value Should Equal     ${body}         /errors/0/message       	 "External ID cannot be blank"
    Json Value Should Equal     ${body}         /errors/0/reason_desc        "External ID cannot be blank"

    [Tags]

    ...                                     name="${CREATIVE_NAME}_VIDEO0101"
    CREATIVE POST Request for Creative      uri=video
    ...                                     JSON=${data}
    ...                                     expected_status_code=200
    Set Suite Variable                          ${videoCreativeId1}         ${DTO_id}
    # Upload File And Attach Request              id=${videoCreativeId1}      type=video               filetype=video     filename=Excercise.mp4       expected_status_code=200

    Create ad for Video                         adgroupId=${videoAdgroupId1}           creativeId=${videoCreativeId1}      videoType=1
    ...                        name="${CREATIVE_NAME}_VIDEO0101"
    Update ad for Video    name="${CREATIVE_NAME}_VIDEO0101"
    Json Value Should Equal     ${body}         /success            true
    Json Value Should Equal     ${body}         /reason_desc        "Success"

    ...                                     adName="${CREATIVE_NAME}_BANNER1901"
    CREATIVE POST Request for Creative      uri=banner
    ...                                     JSON=${data}
    ...                                     expected_status_code=200
    Set Suite Variable                          ${bannerCreativeId1}         ${DTO_id}
    Create ad for Banner               adgroupId=${bannerAdgroupId1}        creativeId=${bannerCreativeId1}       adName="${CREATIVE_NAME}_BANNER1901"      bannerType=0
    Update ad for Banner    adName="${CREATIVE_NAME}_BANNER1901"
    ...       optOutIconLocation="tr"
    ...                                 expected_status_code=200
    Json Value Should Equal     ${body}         /success            true
    Json Value Should Equal     ${body}         /reason_desc        "Success"
    [Tags]

    ...                                     JSON=${data}

    Create ad for Banner               adgroupId=${bannerAdgroupId1}        creativeId=${bannerCreativeId1}       adName="${CREATIVE_NAME}_BANNER2101"      bannerType=0
    ...                                 auth=${QA_CATALINA_AUTH}
    Update ad for Banner                 adName="${CREATIVE_NAME}_BANNER2101"           adgroupId=${bannerAdgroupId1_CAT}
    ...     auth=${QA_CATALINA_AUTH}   expected_status_code=200
    Json Value Should Equal     ${body}         /success            true
    Json Value Should Equal     ${body}         /reason_desc        "Success"
    [Tags]
